	#March to the *Capital*
	focus = {
		id = HUN1933_march_to_the_capital
		icon = GFX_focus_eng_move_to_secure_the_dominions
		x = 7
		y = 2
		relative_position_id = HUN1933_the_will_of_the_people
		cost = 5

		}

		}

		}

				}

			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = fascism }
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						fascism < 0.60
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								ideology = ROOT
								size = 0.5
							}
						}
						50 = {
							country_event = {
								id = ww2tree.10
								days = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						fascism > 0.59
						fascism < 0.70
					}
					random_list = {
						40 = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								ideology = ROOT
								size = 0.4
							}
						}
						60 = {
							country_event = {
								id = ww2tree.10
								days = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						fascism > 0.69
						fascism < 0.80
					}
					random_list = {
						30 = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								ideology = ROOT
								size = 0.3
							}
						}
						70 = {
							country_event = {
								id = ww2tree.10
								days = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						fascism > 0.79
						fascism < 0.90
					}
					random_list = {
						20 = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								ideology = ROOT
								size = 0.2
							}
						}
						80 = {
							country_event = {
								id = ww2tree.10
								days = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						fascism > 0.89
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ruling_party = fascism
								ideology = ROOT
								size = 0.1
							}
						}
						90 = {
							country_event = {
								id = ww2tree.10
								days = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = industrial_complex
										size > 0
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {

						NOT = {

						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
